The ISO 8601 standard for date and time representation defines a format that includes the following elements:
- Year: represented by four digits (YYYY)
- Month: represented by two digits (MM)
- Day: represented by two digits (DD)
- Time: represented by two digits for hours (HH), followed by two digits for minutes (MM), and optionally followed by two digits for seconds (SS)
- Timezone: represented by a positive or negative offset from UTC, indicated by a plus (+) or minus (-) sign, followed by two digits for hours (HH) and two digits for minutes (MM)
